 ' Bharti Airtel has blamed Reliance Jio itself for network connectivity issues and call drop
 airtel ne kaha ki isaki vajah yah he ki jeeyo kii taiyaariyaan adhuri hai tathaa usne paryaapt pareekshan nahin kiya or shuruyaat se pehle ke charan main hi badi sankhya main graahak jod liye
 In a letter to Reliance Jio, Airtel said, "reliance Jio is citing insufficient Point of Interconnection (POI) as the reason for the large number of calls failing, but we believe that the main reason for such call failure is that the company a large number of customers were added before the commercial operations were announced
 ' yah patr kal bheja gaya
 The letter said that according to the actual communication movement, it is necessary for the POI that other parties should also take necessary steps
 'yahaan yah ullekhneey he ki hamaare behatar prayaason ke baavjood pioai abhi vistaar ke charan main he or isaki vajah aapaki taraf uthe mudde hai
 Comments airtel ne kaha ki uski ore se twarit prayaason ke baavjood aaj kii taarikh tak uplabdh karaae gaye 3,048 pioai main se sirf 2,484 interconect port chaalu hai
 The reason for this is that the preparations of Reliance Jio are incomplete and its testing team is not competent
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) reliance jeeyo ko likhe patr main airtel ne kaha, 'reliance jeeyo badi sankhya main kol vifal hone kii vajah aparyaapt point of interconection (pioai) bataa rahi he, lekin hamaara maananaa he ki is tarah kii kol vifaltaa kii pramukh vajah yah he ki company ne vanijyik parichaalan kii ghoshnaa se pehle hi badi sankhya main graahak jod liye
 'this letter was sent yesterday
 patr main kaha gaya he ki vaastavik sanchaar avaagaman ke hisaab se pioai ke liye jaruri he anya paksh bhi jaruri kadam uthaaen
 'it is worth mentioning here that despite our better efforts, the POI is still in the phase of expansion and the reason for this is the issues arising on your side

 usne paise anth kar surajeet ko afghanistan bhejne kaa vaada kiya lekin pahunchaa diya dubai
 According to Surjit's brother Omprakash, Surjeet spent three months in Dubai very difficult in 2013
 surajeet yahi intjaar karata rahaa ki ek din use afghanistan bheja jayega
 In an expensive city like Dubai, how could Surjit spend more days with limited money
 thak haar kar wo bharat laut aayaa
 After coming to India, he caught the travel agent along with the family
 omprakash kii maane to travel agent ne maamle ko sulajhane ke liye surajeet ko kuwait bhejne kii peshkash kii
 Also demanded 45,000 rupees more
 surajeet phir jhaanse main aa gaya
 This time he was sent to Iraq instead of Kuwait
 ise bhi padhein : iraq se laae gaye bharatiyon ke avshesh, punjab sarkaar degi har parivaar ke ek sadsy ko naukariomprakash ne bataaya ki surajeet iraq se lagaataar phone par bataata rahata tha ki vahaan kitne mushkil halaat hai
 Surjit was taken to Iraq, for driving but forcibly paid labor
 kaam na karne par bhookha rakh kar sajaa di jaati
 Hearing Surjit's distress, Omprakash and the rest of the family asked him to return to India
 surajeet kaa us par yahi jawaab hota ki vahaan ke jaise halaat hai usamen laut aana bhi mumkin nahin he
 Surjeet last called his brother Omprakash in June 2014
 surajeet ne us kol main kaha tha ki use nahin pataa ki wo kabhi jinda ghar laut bhi sakegaa yaa nahin
 Surjeet had also sent a video which itself testified to the explosive situation in Iraq at that time
 us video main ek imaarat se kaala dhuaan uthne ke saath dhamaake saaf sunai dete hai
 Similar to Jalandhar's Surjeet, there is also a story of the remaining 26 people from Punjab whose remains were brought from Mosul, Iraq
 ise bhi padhein : iraq se avshesh to laut aayaa par pita ko nahin dekh pai betiitana sab jaanane-sunne ke baad bhi jalandhar ke naujavaanon kaa kahana he ki ve jaan daanv par laga kar bhi videsh jane ko taiyaar hai
 They also explain the reason for this
 vajah he berogari or parivaar ke liye 2 june kii roti jutaney kii phikr
 According to Surjit's brother Omprakash, there is so much unemployment in his area that if people do, what else should they do? These people are ready to take all kinds of danger to save children from hunger
 berozegaar yuva kehete hai ki roji roti ke liye ve abhi bhi iraq ho yaa or koi khadi desh, jane se parhez nahin karenge
 They are compelled to do so to feed the family and to repay the debt
 surajeet ke gaanv adampur main hi rahane vaale devendra palkuwaitise haal main hi vatan laute hai
 According to Devendra, he lived in Kuwait for about one and a half years
 jahaan devendra kaam karte the wo jagah pehle iraq main hi thi lekin baad main us par kuwait kaa niyantran ho gaya
 According to Devendra, human skeletons also appeared to him several times during his work there
 kai baar jinda bam bhi vahaan mili
 According to Devendra, he had to return due to important household chores
 devendra kaa kahana he ki unhen phir mauka mila to wo iraq to nahin, kuwait yaa or kisi khadi desh main chale jaaenge
 Because it is helplessness, will take it wherever it wants
 haalanki devendra ye bhi kehete hai ki ab pehle se vahaan halaat sudhare hai
 Rocky living in Adampur is unemployed
 padhai puri karne ke baad wo naukari karne ke liye khadi deshon main janaa chahta tha
 But after knowing what happened to Indians like Surjit in Mosul, Rocky has given up his intention to move out of the country
 rocky ke mutabik wo yahi rah kar mehnat mazdooree se roti kamayega
 Also read: VK Singh, who brought the bodies of 38 Indians, said, giving compensation is not like distributing biscuits
 Charanjit of Adampur has worked in Kuwait for 7-8 years
 charanjit ke mutabik kuwait main rahete hue unhen iraq ke bure halaat kaa pataa chalata rahata tha
 Charanjeet says that conditions are fine in Kuwait, so he would like to go there again
 charanjit ne saath hi kaha ki khadi desh main naukari ke liye jane se pehle gharavaalon ko samajhaana padataa he
 According to Charanjeet, there is no option but to go there
 yahaan desh main unke liye aisa koi kaam nahin jisase ki itnaa kamaaya ja sake ki parivaar kaa acchhee tarah guzaara ho jaae
 Charanjeet also believes that due to working in the Gulf country, his family always cares for him
 aise main ve hameshaa apane parivaar ko himmat dete rahete hai
 Leaders of Punjab also believe that under which circumstances the youth of the state have to migrate to the Gulf countries
 lekin yahaan bhi ve raajnneetik aarope-pratyaropon se nahin chookte
 Akali Dal MLA Pawan Singh Tinu from Jalandhar blames the system for the migration of youth
 ab ye baat duusari he ki isi system kaa wo haal tak hissaa rahe
 Tinu says that government policies are not in favor of the poor, even if they were in favor of the poor, even after 70 years of independence, the youth would not have to go to the Gulf countries due to unemployment
 tinu ye kehane se bhi nahin chookte ki unhone akali dal ke raaj main 2 lakh logon ko sarkari naukari di lekin uske pehle rahi congress sarkaar sirf 27 hajaar logon ko sarkari naukari de saki
 Politics keeps going its way but it is a reality that no one is worried about unemployed youth

 Even knowing this, there may be danger to life
 lekin parivaar kaa pet bharne kaa sawaal saamne hota he to ve is khatre kii bhi parvaah nahin karte

 pahalwaan ko bhi javaani main padi lathi budhaape kii sardiyon tak dard detii he

 to chaliye, aaj kahani sunaate hai lathi kii
 Police sticks
 kisi karnal kaa danda nahin, sangh kaa dand nahin, harvaahe kii lagghi nahin
 
 
 Police sticks iske police kaa hathiyaar banane kii shuruyaat se aadhunik or faishanebuk hone tak kaa safar
 Lathiyandesh is often seen by police to protest against the Citizenship Amendment Act (CAA) and NRC (NRC)
 is dauraan kanoon vyavastha banaae rakhane or bheed ko kaabo karne ke liye police lathi charge kar rahi he
 The crowd is controlled by lathi sticks
 ek se ek atyaadhunik hathiyaar hone ke baavjood lathi yani bent kaa istemaal police zyada karti he
 Police cane is not a common stick
 balki ise vishesh rup se banaaya jaataa he
 Not only this, training is also given from policemen to officers to run it
 britishkaal se ho rahaa he istemaalajab bharat main angrejon kaa shashan tha, to ve bharatiyon par bahut julm jyaadati karte the
 Used every means to collect taxes
 swatantraaa sangram main shaamil logon kii bheed ko kaabo karne ke liye lathi dandon kaa istemaal karte the
 Since then, the practice of lathi came in the police
 ise banane ke liye thos lakdi nahin balki lacheelee bent kaa istemaal hota tha
 Alok Prasad, former Uttar Pradesh Director General of Police and currently a member of UPSC, says that cane has been used in the police since the British era
 bent lacheela hota he
 Its blow does not cause fracture
 iskaa makasad kisi ko nuksaan pahunchaana nahin hota
 The aim is to get hurt but do not cause great harm
 ise police kaa ek maanviya pahalu bhi kah sakate hai

e
 lathi is also an important part of right control drill

 aksar dhad se neeche pairon ke peeche kii taraf lathi maari jaati he
 The real aim is to disperse the crowd
 unhone bataaya ki rashtriya police academy main ipies adhikariyon ko bhi bent chalaane kii training di jaati he
 Lathis are made in Muzaffarnagar, cane or sticks are made in Muzaffarnagar district of Uttar Pradesh
 is jile main kai parivaar varshon se bent banane kaa kaam karte aa rahe hai
 Cane makers prepare cane and sticks by heating bamboo in fire furnaces
 muzaffarnagar ke gaushala road bent banane vaale kai kaarkaane maujuud hai
 Bamboo is sourced from Bihar and Assam to make cane
 kaarkaanon bans ko saaf kar aag main tapaaya jaataa he
 Then they are made beautiful by coloring them
 mirzapur kii bent bhi kam nahinupi ke hi mirzapur kii bent yaa lathi bhi kaaphi mashhoor he
 Which is sent to Nepal
 mirzapur ke kushiyara or elahabaad ke manda ke jangalon main ek khaas tarah ke bans paae jate hai
 Canes are also made after hard work from them
 jaankaron ke mutabik bans kii koth main lakdi tedi-medhi hoti he
 Then the artisans clean it for a long time
 bent ko sidhaa karte hai

 tab jaakar bent taiyaar hoti he

 Citizenship Law introduced in Lok Sabha, Union Home Minister Amit Shah introduced many parties including Bill Congress, protesting Article 370, after NRC, now Modi government is another big bet
 kendriya grih mantri amit shah ne somvaar ko loksabhaa main naagarikta sanshodhan bill ko pesh kiya
 Under this bill, the rules regarding the citizenship granted to the refugees who enter the country will be completely changed
 centre sarkaar ke is kanoon kaa vipakshi partiyaan virodh kar rahi hai or ise bharat ke mul niyamon ke khilaaf bataa rahi hai
 What is disputed in this bill, what was there before and what is going to happen now
 jaane bill se judi 10 baaten
 
 
 1
 modi sarkaar jo nayaa bill laa rahi he, use citijan amendament bill, 2019 naam diya gaya he
 The introduction of this bill will change the Citizens Act, 1955
 2
 Under the Modi government's bill, it has been said to give citizenship of India to Hindu, Sikh, Buddhist, Jain, Parsi and Christian refugees coming from Afghanistan, Bangladesh, Pakistan
 3
 Also, all these refugees will not be treated as illegal citizens in India
 abhi ke kanoon ke tahat bharat main avaidh tareeke se aae logon ko unke desh waapas bhejne yaa phir hiraasat main lene kii baat he
 4
 in sabhi sharnaarthiyon ko bharat main ab naagarikta paane ke liye kam se kam 6 saal kaa vakt bitaana hoga
 Earlier this deadline was for 11 years
 5
 Inner line permit areas of Arunachal Pradesh, Nagaland and Mizoram have been excluded from this bill
 iske alaava ye bill north east ke chathe shedul kaa bhi bachaav karata he
 Read the full coverage related to the citizenship bill by clicking here
 
 
 6
 According to the new law, any Hindu, Jain, Sikh, Buddhist, Christian citizen from afghanistan-bangladesh-pakistan who came to India before December 31, 2014 will not be considered as illegal citizen
 7
 Whichever of these citizens is an OCI holder, if he has violated any law, he will be given a chance to speak once
 8
 Opposition parties are opposing this bill and calling it a violation of the Constitution of India
 vipaksh kaa kahana he ki centre sarkaar jo bill laa rahi he, vah desh main dharm ke aadhaar par bantwaaraa karegaa jo samanta ke adhikaar ke khilaaf he
 9
 purvottar main is bill kaa sabase adhik virodh ho rahaa he, purvottar ke logon kaa maananaa he kibangladesh se adhiktar hindu aakar assam, arunachal, manipurajaise rajyon main basate hai aise main ye purvottar rajyon ke liye thik nahin rahegaa
 Many student organizations, political parties in the Northeast are against it
 10
 The Asom Gana Parishad, a partner of the Bharatiya Janata Party in the NDA, has also opposed the bill, which broke away from the coalition when the bill entered the Lok Sabha
 haalanki, kaarykaal khatm hone par jab bill khatm hua to vah waapas bhi ai
